SI unit: dimensionless

Resonant build-up: A ∝ Q
SI unit: m

SI unit: rad

SI unit: dimensionless

SI unit: s

Doppler Effect
Moving observer: f' = f (c ± vo) / c
SI unit: Hz

Moving source: f' = f c / (c ∓ vs)
SI unit: Hz

General Doppler shift: f' = f (c ± vo) / (c ∓ vs)
SI unit: Hz

Approaching source: f' increases
SI unit: Hz

Receding source: f' decreases
SI unit: Hz

Approaching observer: f' increases
SI unit: Hz

Radial velocity: vr = v cos θ
SI unit: m/s

Doppler with radial source: f' = f c / (c - vr)
SI unit: Hz

Doppler with radial observer: f' = f (c + vr) / c
SI unit: Hz

Mach cone condition: M > 1
SI unit: dimensionless

Shock angle: sin μ = c / v
SI unit: rad

Sonic boom cone: μ = arcsin(1 / M)
SI unit: rad

Astronomical redshift: z = (λobs - λrest) / λrest
SI unit: dimensionless

Frequency shift: Δf = f' - f
SI unit: Hz

Approximate shift: Δf / f ≈ vr / c
SI unit: dimensionless

Small-velocity Doppler: f' ≈ f(1 ± v / c)
SI unit: Hz

Moving boundary reflection: f' = f (c ± vb) / (c ∓ vb)
SI unit: Hz

Velocity of sound source: vs
SI unit: m/s

Velocity of observer: vo
SI unit: m/s

Source approach: vs positive toward observer
SI unit: m/s

Observer approach: vo positive toward source
SI unit: m/s

Echo Doppler: fecho = f' after reflection
SI unit: Hz

Radar-like speed estimate: v ≈ c Δf / 2f
SI unit: m/s

Frequency ratio: f'/f
SI unit: dimensionless

Cosine angle factor: vr = v cos θ
SI unit: m/s

Reflection and Refraction of Sound
Reflection law: θi = θr
SI unit: rad

Normal incidence reflection: θi = 0
SI unit: rad

Transmission coefficient: T = It / Ii
SI unit: dimensionless

Reflection coefficient: R = Ir / Ii
SI unit: dimensionless

Energy balance: R + T = 1
SI unit: dimensionless

Acoustic impedance mismatch: Z₁ ≠ Z₂
SI unit: Pa · s/m

Normal incidence reflection: R = (Z₂ - Z₁)² / (Z₂ + Z₁)²
SI unit: dimensionless

Normal incidence transmission: T = 4Z₁Z₂ / (Z₁ + Z₂)²
SI unit: dimensionless

Snell law for sound: sin θ₁ / c₁ = sin θ₂ / c₂
SI unit: dimensionless

Refraction angle: θ₂ = arcsin((c₂ / c₁) sin θ₁)
SI unit: rad

Bending toward slow medium: θ decreases when c decreases
SI unit: rad

Critical angle: sin θc = c₁ / c₂
SI unit: dimensionless

Total internal reflection: θi > θc
SI unit: rad

Phase reversal at rigid wall: p' reflected with sign change
SI unit: Pa

Free end reflection: displacement reflection without sign change
SI unit: m

Hard boundary pressure antinode: p' max at wall
SI unit: Pa

Soft boundary pressure node: p' = 0
SI unit: Pa

Angle of incidence: θi
SI unit: rad

Angle of reflection: θr
SI unit: rad

Transmission angle: θt
SI unit: rad

Speed ratio: c₂ / c₁
SI unit: dimensionless

Refraction index for sound: n = c₀ / c
SI unit: dimensionless

Impedance refraction relation: Z = ρc
SI unit: Pa · s/m

Layered medium travel time: t = d / c
SI unit: s
